THE LAND ACQUISITION ACT (CHAPTER 460)
Declaration Under Section 5
I, Janaka Bandara Thennakoon, Minister of Lands and Land
Development hereby declare, under Sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the
Land Acquisition Act, that the lands described below are needed for a
public purpose and will be acquired under the provisions of that Act.
Seven Hundred and Ninety Three (793)  allotments of land in
total Extent of about 0.1161 Hectare, depicted in Advance Tracing
No.KA/MTG/12/216 prepared by the Surveyor-General, situated
in the Villages of Mathugma, Horawala, Welipenna, Leuwwanduwa,
Munamalewatta in the Divisional Secretary’s Division of
Mathugama, in the District of Kalutara and bounded as follows:
1. Lot No.69 – Katupiliyagodakuruduwatta – Extent: 0.0014
Hectare
North: Road (R.D.A); East:  Road (R.D.A); South:  Lot No. 70
and Katupiliyagodakuruduwatta claimed by P.W. Ashoka Dharmasiri
and P .W. Sarath Wimalaweera; West: Katupiliyagodakuruduwatta
claimed by P.W. Sarath Wimalaweera.
